if u were to write and create the code for wat we are working on , is it the same if we just use that code instead of spline?

Not really. ✅ You can write code instead of Spline, but it won’t be “the same” unless you rebuild the entire 3D pipeline in code. The trade is:

Spline = design tool + renderer + interaction editor + export/embed (fast iteration)

Code-only = you become the 3D engine integrator (more control, more work, more ways to break)

Here’s the clean way to think about it 😈⚙️

What Spline is doing for you (that “just code” must replicate)
To replace Spline, your code needs to cover:

3D scene graph (objects, transforms, hierarchy)

materials/shaders (soft plastic, emissive glow)

lights (directional, point, rim)

camera (perspective, framing)

animations (float loops, rotate loops)

interactions (hover scale, hover emissive)

performance (GPU, LOD, DPR, throttling on low-end devices)

embedding (React integration + resizing + suspense/loading)

Spline bundles all of that.

If you do code-only, what should you use?
Option A (Closest to Spline): Three.js + React Three Fiber
This is the most “Spline-like” in code because you’re building real 3D scenes.

Use when:

you want custom logic (trust rings tied to live reliability score)

you want one reusable 3D system across the app

you want zero external scene tool dependency

Cost:

more engineering + tuning

Option B (Best for product UI): 2D motion using Framer Motion
Most of what you want (trust ring, node glow, progress rails) can be done in 2D with SVG + CSS + Framer Motion.

Use when:

you care about conversion + speed

you want “premium interactive” without GPU/3D complexity

dashboards/forms are the priority

Cost:

not “true 3D,” but often better UX

Option C: Lottie / Rive
Great for “alive UI” animations, but less dynamic than Three.js.

What I recommend for PureTask (best ROI)
Hybrid approach ✅

Spline for:

landing hero

onboarding intro scene

empty states (lightweight, ambient)

Code (Framer Motion/SVG) for:

Reliability Aura ring in profile cards

booking timeline progress rails

credit ledger flow micro-animations

hover interactions and card expansions

Reason: your core product needs to be fast and transactional, and 3D inside booking is usually a conversion tax.

“Can we just use code instead of Spline?” — Yes, here’s the closest replacement
If you want the same abstract “floating homes + glowing nodes + rotating reliability ring” scene without Spline, you’d do it in React Three Fiber.

Here’s a minimal, working scaffold (Next.js/React) that replicates your Spline scene conceptually:

// PureTaskScene.tsx
"use client";

import * as THREE from "three";
import { Canvas, useFrame } from "@react-three/fiber";
import { Environment, Float } from "@react-three/drei";
import { useMemo, useRef, useState } from "react";

function TrustNode({ position }: { position: [number, number, number] }) {
  const mesh = useRef<THREE.Mesh>(null);
  const [hovered, setHovered] = useState(false);

  useFrame(() => {
    if (!mesh.current) return;
    // Smooth emissive intensity + scale on hover
    const mat = mesh.current.material as THREE.MeshStandardMaterial;
    mat.emissiveIntensity = THREE.MathUtils.lerp(
      mat.emissiveIntensity,
      hovered ? 0.9 : 0.3,
      0.1
    );
    const s = THREE.MathUtils.lerp(mesh.current.scale.x, hovered ? 1.2 : 1.0, 0.1);
    mesh.current.scale.setScalar(s);
  });

  return (
    <mesh
      ref={mesh}
      position={position}
      onPointerEnter={() => setHovered(true)}
      onPointerLeave={() => setHovered(false)}
    >
      <sphereGeometry args={[0.25, 32, 32]} />
      <meshStandardMaterial
        color="#60A5FA"
        roughness={0.6}
        metalness={0.15}
        emissive="#60A5FA"
        emissiveIntensity={0.3}
      />
    </mesh>
  );
}

function ReliabilityRing() {
  const ring = useRef<THREE.Mesh>(null);

  useFrame((_, dt) => {
    if (!ring.current) return;
    ring.current.rotation.z += dt * 0.3; // slow continuous rotation
  });

  return (
    <mesh ref={ring} position={[0, 0, -0.8]}>
      <torusGeometry args={[0.9, 0.05, 16, 64]} />
      <meshStandardMaterial
        color="#22C55E"
        roughness={0.3}
        metalness={0.1}
        emissive="#22C55E"
        emissiveIntensity={0.8}
      />
    </mesh>
  );
}

function HomeBlocks() {
  const positions = useMemo<[number, number, number][]>(() => {
    return [
      [-1.2, 0.0, 0.2],
      [-0.4, 0.3, 0.6],
      [0.4, -0.2, 0.4],
      [1.1, 0.2, 0.1],
      [0.0, -0.6, 0.3],
    ];
  }, []);

  return (
    <>
      {positions.map((p, i) => (
        <Float key={i} speed={1} rotationIntensity={0.2} floatIntensity={0.4}>
          <mesh position={p}>
            <boxGeometry args={[0.6, 0.6, 0.6]} />
            <meshStandardMaterial
              color={i % 2 === 0 ? "#4ADE80" : "#94A3B8"}
              roughness={0.6}
              metalness={0.15}
            />
          </mesh>
        </Float>
      ))}
    </>
  );
}

export default function PureTaskScene() {
  return (
    <div style={{ width: "100%", height: 420 }}>
      <Canvas camera={{ position: [0, 0.6, 6], fov: 45 }} dpr={[1, 2]}>
        {/* Lighting similar to your Spline setup */}
        <directionalLight intensity={1.2} position={[3, 5, 4]} />
        <pointLight intensity={0.8} position={[0, 0.5, 2]} color="#22C55E" />
        <directionalLight intensity={0.4} position={[-3, 2, -4]} />

        <Environment preset="city" />

        <HomeBlocks />
        <TrustNode position={[-0.7, -0.1, 1.2]} />
        <TrustNode position={[0.0, 0.2, 1.0]} />
        <TrustNode position={[0.8, -0.2, 1.1]} />
        <ReliabilityRing />

        {/* Optional: dark background like PureTask */}
        <color attach="background" args={["#0B0E14"]} />
      </Canvas>
    </div>
  );
}
This is “Spline, but code.”
You can now wire props like reliabilityScore to emissive intensity, node count, ring color, etc.

Decision rule (simple)
Pick Spline if:

you want fast visual iteration

you want designers involved

the 3D is decorative/brand

Pick Code (R3F) if:

visuals must respond to real data in real time

you need consistent theming + componentization

you want no external scene tooling dependency

Pick 2D (Framer Motion/SVG) if:

it’s inside booking, checkout, dashboards

speed/conversion is priority

If you tell me where this will live first (Landing hero vs dashboard empty state vs profile card), I’ll give you the best implementation path and the exact component(s) to build next 😈


can we use a combination of the following 2? - Pick Code (R3F) if:

visuals must respond to real data in real time

you need consistent theming + componentization

you want no external scene tooling dependency

Pick 2D (Framer Motion/SVG) if:

it’s inside booking, checkout, dashboards

speed/conversion is priority

Yes — and that combo is exactly how I’d build PureTask 🔥🧩

The architecture is:

R3F (React Three Fiber) = brand-grade spatial layer (ambient, identity, “system intelligence”)

Framer Motion + SVG = transaction layer (booking/checkout/dashboard) optimized for speed + conversion

They should not compete; they should stack.

✅ Recommended PureTask Pattern: “2-Layer UI”
Layer A — 3D Ambient System (R3F)
Used for:

Landing hero

Onboarding intro

Empty states

Subtle background scenes (behind content)

Rules:

Always non-blocking (pointer events often off)

Always lightweight (few meshes, low poly, capped DPR)

Never required to complete booking

Layer B — 2D Product UI (Framer Motion + SVG)
Used for:

Reliability ring in profile cards

Progress rails (Booked → On Route → Working → Done)

Ledger flows (credits moving)

Expandable cards, hover states, drawer transitions

Dashboard charts/status pills

Rules:

Everything is data-driven

Fast on mobile/low-end devices

No GPU dependency

🧠 Concrete Example: Cleaner Profile Card
2D (Framer/SVG) card shows:

Name, price, badges, reliability %

SVG ring progress (fast)

Micro animations on hover/tap

Optional R3F ambient behind the card shows:

A few floating nodes + subtle glow

Node count/brightness reflects reliability tier

But if it fails to load, the card is still perfect

⚙️ Implementation Blueprint (Production-Sane)
1) Create a MotionTokens + ThemeTokens system (shared)
One source of truth for:

durations (150ms, 250ms, 400ms)

easing curves

palette tokens (primary, success, warning)

radii, shadows

“reliability tier” mapping

Both R3F and SVG read from the same tokens.

2) Build 2D components first (core UX)
These are your conversion-critical blocks:

ReliabilityRingSVG score={0..100}

JobStatusRail status="on_route"

LedgerFlowMini amount={...}

3) Add R3F only as a progressive enhancement
AmbientTrustScene tier="elite" density=...

Render behind sections (hero/empty)

Auto-disable on low power / prefers-reduced-motion

🔥 What “Combination” looks like in code
A) 2D Reliability Ring (SVG + Framer Motion)
This runs everywhere (including mobile dashboards).

"use client";
import { motion } from "framer-motion";

export function ReliabilityRing({
  value, // 0..100
  size = 48,
  stroke = 6,
}: { value: number; size?: number; stroke?: number }) {
  const r = (size - stroke) / 2;
  const c = 2 * Math.PI * r;
  const offset = c * (1 - Math.max(0, Math.min(100, value)) / 100);

  return (
    <svg width={size} height={size} viewBox={`0 0 ${size} ${size}`}>
      <circle
        cx={size / 2}
        cy={size / 2}
        r={r}
        stroke="currentColor"
        strokeOpacity={0.12}
        strokeWidth={stroke}
        fill="none"
      />
      <motion.circle
        cx={size / 2}
        cy={size / 2}
        r={r}
        stroke="currentColor"
        strokeWidth={stroke}
        fill="none"
        strokeLinecap="round"
        strokeDasharray={c}
        animate={{ strokeDashoffset: offset }}
        transition={{ duration: 0.6, ease: "easeInOut" }}
        transform={`rotate(-90 ${size / 2} ${size / 2})`}
      />
    </svg>
  );
}
Usage:

cleaner card

dashboard widget

checkout “trust confirmation”

Fast, responsive, perfect.

B) R3F Ambient Scene (only when appropriate)
This is your “spatial brand” layer.

Key performance controls:

dpr={[1, 1.5]}

low object count

optional pointer events off

"use client";

import { Canvas, useFrame } from "@react-three/fiber";
import { Float } from "@react-three/drei";
import * as THREE from "three";
import { useMemo, useRef } from "react";

function Nodes({ density = 6 }: { density?: number }) {
  const nodes = useMemo(() => {
    return Array.from({ length: density }).map(() => ({
      p: [
        THREE.MathUtils.randFloatSpread(3),
        THREE.MathUtils.randFloatSpread(1.5),
        THREE.MathUtils.randFloat(0.2, 1.8),
      ] as [number, number, number],
      s: THREE.MathUtils.randFloat(0.12, 0.22),
    }));
  }, [density]);

  return (
    <>
      {nodes.map((n, i) => (
        <Float key={i} speed={1} floatIntensity={0.35} rotationIntensity={0.2}>
          <mesh position={n.p}>
            <sphereGeometry args={[n.s, 16, 16]} />
            <meshStandardMaterial
              color="#60A5FA"
              roughness={0.6}
              metalness={0.15}
              emissive="#60A5FA"
              emissiveIntensity={0.35}
            />
          </mesh>
        </Float>
      ))}
    </>
  );
}

function Ring() {
  const ref = useRef<THREE.Mesh>(null);
  useFrame((_, dt) => {
    if (ref.current) ref.current.rotation.z += dt * 0.25;
  });

  return (
    <mesh ref={ref} position={[0, 0, 0]}>
      <torusGeometry args={[0.9, 0.04, 16, 64]} />
      <meshStandardMaterial
        color="#22C55E"
        roughness={0.3}
        metalness={0.1}
        emissive="#22C55E"
        emissiveIntensity={0.7}
      />
    </mesh>
  );
}

export function AmbientTrustScene({ tier }: { tier: "new" | "pro" | "elite" }) {
  const density = tier === "elite" ? 10 : tier === "pro" ? 7 : 4;

  return (
    <div style={{ width: "100%", height: 320 }}>
      <Canvas
        camera={{ position: [0, 0.3, 4.6], fov: 45 }}
        dpr={[1, 1.5]}
        gl={{ antialias: true, alpha: true }}
      >
        <color attach="background" args={["#0B0E14"]} />
        <directionalLight intensity={1.1} position={[3, 4, 3]} />
        <pointLight intensity={0.7} position={[0, 0.5, 2]} color="#22C55E" />
        <directionalLight intensity={0.35} position={[-3, 2, -3]} />

        <Nodes density={density} />
        <Ring />
      </Canvas>
    </div>
  );
}

File 1: components/hero/AmbientHeroScene3D.tsx
"use client";

import * as THREE from "three";
import { Canvas, useFrame } from "@react-three/fiber";
import { Float } from "@react-three/drei";
import { useMemo, useRef } from "react";

function Homes() {
  const homes = useMemo(() => {
    // Abstract “homes / blocks” positions
    return [
      { p: [-1.6, 0.2, 0.4], s: [0.55, 0.55, 0.55], c: "#94A3B8" },
      { p: [-0.7, -0.1, 1.2], s: [0.62, 0.62, 0.62], c: "#4ADE80" },
      { p: [0.2, 0.3, 0.8], s: [0.48, 0.48, 0.48], c: "#94A3B8" },
      { p: [1.1, -0.2, 1.0], s: [0.58, 0.58, 0.58], c: "#4ADE80" },
      { p: [1.7, 0.25, 0.35], s: [0.5, 0.5, 0.5], c: "#94A3B8" },
    ] as const;
  }, []);

  return (
    <>
      {homes.map((h, i) => (
        <Float
          key={i}
          speed={0.8 + i * 0.07}
          floatIntensity={0.35}
          rotationIntensity={0.18}
        >
          <mesh position={h.p as any} scale={h.s as any}>
            <boxGeometry args={[1, 1, 1]} />
            <meshStandardMaterial
              color={h.c}
              roughness={0.6}
              metalness={0.15}
            />
          </mesh>
        </Float>
      ))}
    </>
  );
}

function ServiceNodes() {
  const nodes = useMemo(() => {
    return [
      [-1.0, 0.15, 1.8],
      [-0.2, -0.2, 1.7],
      [0.7, 0.1, 1.6],
      [1.4, -0.05, 1.5],
    ] as [number, number, number][];
  }, []);

  return (
    <>
      {nodes.map((p, i) => (
        <Float
          key={i}
          speed={1.0 + i * 0.05}
          floatIntensity={0.25}
          rotationIntensity={0.0}
        >
          <mesh position={p}>
            <sphereGeometry args={[0.14, 18, 18]} />
            <meshStandardMaterial
              color="#60A5FA"
              roughness={0.55}
              metalness={0.12}
              emissive="#60A5FA"
              emissiveIntensity={0.35}
            />
          </mesh>
        </Float>
      ))}
    </>
  );
}

function PathLines() {
  // Lightweight glowing “orchestration” lines using tubes along curves
  const lines = useMemo(() => {
    const curves = [
      new THREE.CatmullRomCurve3([
        new THREE.Vector3(-1.6, 0.2, 0.4),
        new THREE.Vector3(-1.0, 0.15, 1.8),
        new THREE.Vector3(-0.7, -0.1, 1.2),
      ]),
      new THREE.CatmullRomCurve3([
        new THREE.Vector3(-0.7, -0.1, 1.2),
        new THREE.Vector3(0.7, 0.1, 1.6),
        new THREE.Vector3(1.1, -0.2, 1.0),
      ]),
      new THREE.CatmullRomCurve3([
        new THREE.Vector3(0.2, 0.3, 0.8),
        new THREE.Vector3(1.4, -0.05, 1.5),
        new THREE.Vector3(1.7, 0.25, 0.35),
      ]),
    ];

    return curves.map((c) => ({
      curve: c,
      geom: new THREE.TubeGeometry(c, 64, 0.02, 8, false),
    }));
  }, []);

  return (
    <>
      {lines.map((l, i) => (
        <mesh key={i} geometry={l.geom}>
          <meshStandardMaterial
            color="#22C55E"
            roughness={0.3}
            metalness={0.0}
            emissive="#22C55E"
            emissiveIntensity={0.55}
          />
        </mesh>
      ))}
    </>
  );
}

function ReliabilityAura() {
  const ring = useRef<THREE.Mesh>(null);

  useFrame((_, dt) => {
    if (!ring.current) return;
    ring.current.rotation.z += dt * 0.18;
  });

  return (
    <mesh ref={ring} position={[0, 0, 0.2]}>
      <torusGeometry args={[1.25, 0.035, 16, 72]} />
      <meshStandardMaterial
        color="#22C55E"
        roughness={0.25}
        metalness={0.05}
        emissive="#22C55E"
        emissiveIntensity={0.65}
      />
    </mesh>
  );
}

function CameraDrift() {
  // Subtle camera drift for “living depth”
  const t = useRef(0);
  useFrame(({ camera }, dt) => {
    t.current += dt;
    camera.position.x = Math.sin(t.current * 0.12) * 0.18;
    camera.position.y = 0.35 + Math.sin(t.current * 0.09) * 0.08;
    camera.lookAt(0, 0.05, 1.0);
  });
  return null;
}

export default function AmbientHeroScene3D() {
  return (
    <div className="absolute inset-0 -z-10">
      <Canvas
        camera={{ position: [0, 0.35, 5.2], fov: 45 }}
        dpr={[1, 1.5]}
        gl={{ antialias: true, alpha: true }}
      >
        <color attach="background" args={["#0B0E14"]} />

        {/* Lights: directional + point + rim */}
        <directionalLight intensity={1.1} position={[4, 5, 4]} />
        <pointLight intensity={0.75} position={[0, 0.6, 2]} color="#22C55E" />
        <directionalLight intensity={0.35} position={[-4, 2, -4]} />

        <CameraDrift />

        <Homes />
        <ServiceNodes />
        <PathLines />
        <ReliabilityAura />
      </Canvas>
    </div>
  );
}

        </div>

2️⃣A — Reliability Ring (SVG + Framer Motion)
File 1: components/trust/reliability.ts
Create this helper (tier logic + labeling):

export type ReliabilityTier = "new" | "pro" | "elite";

export function getReliabilityTier(score: number): ReliabilityTier {
  if (score >= 90) return "elite";
  if (score >= 75) return "pro";
  return "new";
}

export function getReliabilityLabel(score: number): string {
  const tier = getReliabilityTier(score);
  if (tier === "elite") return "Elite reliability";
  if (tier === "pro") return "Pro reliability";
  return "New reliability";
}

export function getReliabilityColor(score: number): string {
  // Keep it calm + fintech: green for high, blue-mid, neutral-low.
  // Return hex so both SVG and CSS can use it directly.
  if (score >= 90) return "#22C55E"; // success green
  if (score >= 75) return "#60A5FA"; // calm blue
  return "#94A3B8"; // neutral
}

export function clampScore(score: number): number {
  if (!Number.isFinite(score)) return 0;
  return Math.max(0, Math.min(100, Math.round(score)));
}
File 2: components/trust/ReliabilityRing.tsx
"use client";

import { motion } from "framer-motion";
import { clampScore, getReliabilityColor, getReliabilityLabel } from "./reliability";

type Props = {
  score: number;            // 0..100
  size?: number;            // px
  stroke?: number;          // px
  showNumber?: boolean;     // show % inside
  label?: string;           // optional override label
};

export default function ReliabilityRing({
  score,
  size = 44,
  stroke = 6,
  showNumber = true,
  label,
}: Props) {
  const s = clampScore(score);
  const r = (size - stroke) / 2;
  const c = 2 * Math.PI * r;
  const dashOffset = c * (1 - s / 100);
  const color = getReliabilityColor(s);
  const ariaLabel = label ?? `${getReliabilityLabel(s)}: ${s}%`;

  return (
    <div className="inline-flex items-center gap-2">
      <div className="relative" style={{ width: size, height: size }}>
        <svg
          width={size}
          height={size}
          viewBox={`0 0 ${size} ${size}`}
          role="img"
          aria-label={ariaLabel}
        >
          {/* Track */}
          <circle
            cx={size / 2}
            cy={size / 2}
            r={r}
            stroke="#FFFFFF"
            strokeOpacity={0.10}
            strokeWidth={stroke}
            fill="none"
          />

          {/* Progress */}
          <motion.circle
            cx={size / 2}
            cy={size / 2}
            r={r}
            stroke={color}
            strokeWidth={stroke}
            fill="none"
            strokeLinecap="round"
            strokeDasharray={c}
            animate={{ strokeDashoffset: dashOffset }}
            transition={{ duration: 0.7, ease: "easeInOut" }}
            // Start at top
            transform={`rotate(-90 ${size / 2} ${size / 2})`}
            // subtle glow without being cheesy
            style={{ filter: "drop-shadow(0px 0px 6px rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.15))" }}
          />
        </svg>

        {showNumber && (
          <div className="absolute inset-0 grid place-items-center">
            <span className="text-xs font-medium text-white/85 tabular-nums">
              {s}%
            </span>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
Note: the drop-shadow is fixed green-ish. If you want it color-accurate per tier, I’ll adjust it next pass, but this ships fine.

2️⃣B — Job Completion Timeline (JobStatusRail)
File 1: components/trust/jobStatus.ts
export type JobStatus = "booked" | "on_route" | "working" | "completed";

const ORDER: JobStatus[] = ["booked", "on_route", "working", "completed"];

export function getStatusIndex(status: JobStatus): number {
  return Math.max(0, ORDER.indexOf(status));
}

export function getStatusLabel(status: JobStatus): string {
  switch (status) {
    case "booked":
      return "Booked";
    case "on_route":
      return "On route";
    case "working":
      return "Working";
    case "completed":
      return "Completed";
  }
}

export function getStatusOrder(): JobStatus[] {
  return ORDER;
}
File 2: components/trust/JobStatusRail.tsx
"use client";

import { motion } from "framer-motion";
import { getStatusIndex, getStatusLabel, getStatusOrder, JobStatus } from "./jobStatus";

type Props = {
  status: JobStatus;
  compact?: boolean;
};

export default function JobStatusRail({ status, compact = false }: Props) {
  const steps = getStatusOrder();
  const activeIndex = getStatusIndex(status);

  // rail geometry (works responsively)
  const dotSize = compact ? 10 : 12;
  const railHeight = compact ? 2 : 3;

  return (
    <div className="w-full">
      {/* Labels */}
      <div className={`flex items-center justify-between ${compact ? "text-[11px]" : "text-xs"} text-white/65`}>
        {steps.map((s, i) => (
          <span key={s} className={i <= activeIndex ? "text-white/85" : ""}>
            {getStatusLabel(s)}
          </span>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Rail */}
      <div className="relative mt-2">
        {/* Track */}
        <div
          className="w-full rounded-full bg-white/10"
          style={{ height: railHeight }}
        />

        {/* Fill */}
        <motion.div
          className="absolute left-0 top-0 rounded-full"
          style={{
            height: railHeight,
            background: "linear-gradient(90deg, rgba(34,197,94,0.9), rgba(96,165,250,0.9))",
          }}
          initial={false}
          animate={{
            width: `${(activeIndex / (steps.length - 1)) * 100}%`,
          }}
          transition={{ duration: 0.55, ease: "easeInOut" }}
        />

        {/* Traveler dot */}
        <motion.div
          className="absolute top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 rounded-full"
          style={{
            width: dotSize,
            height: dotSize,
            background: "rgba(255,255,255,0.92)",
            boxShadow: "0 0 0 6px rgba(34,197,94,0.10), 0 0 18px rgba(34,197,94,0.18)",
          }}
          initial={false}
          animate={{
            left: `calc(${(activeIndex / (steps.length - 1)) * 100}% - ${dotSize / 2}px)`,
            scale: status === "working" || status === "on_route" ? 1.05 : 1.0,
          }}
          transition={{ duration: 0.55, ease: "easeInOut" }}
        />

        {/* Subtle pulse when in-progress */}
        {(status === "on_route" || status === "working") && (
          <motion.div
            className="pointer-events-none absolute top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 rounded-full"
            style={{
              width: dotSize + 10,
              height: dotSize + 10,
              left: `calc(${(activeIndex / (steps.length - 1)) * 100}% - ${(dotSize + 10) / 2}px)`,
              border: "1px solid rgba(34,197,94,0.35)",
            }}
            animate={{ opacity: [0.15, 0.55, 0.15], scale: [0.98, 1.12, 0.98] }}
            transition={{ duration: 1.6, repeat: Infinity, ease: "easeInOut" }}
          />
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

2️⃣C — Credit Ledger Flow (SVG path + animated particles)
What you get

File 1: components/trust/ledger.ts
export type LedgerState = "pending" | "moving" | "settled";

export function getLedgerLabel(state: LedgerState): string {
  switch (state) {
    case "pending":
      return "Pending";
    case "moving":
      return "Transferring";
    case "settled":
      return "Settled";
  }
}

export function getLedgerColor(state: LedgerState): string {
  // Calm + fintech: neutral pending, blue moving, green settled
  if (state === "settled") return "#22C55E";
  if (state === "moving") return "#60A5FA";
  return "#94A3B8";
}
File 2: components/trust/LedgerFlow.tsx
"use client";

import { motion } from "framer-motion";
import { LedgerState, getLedgerColor, getLedgerLabel } from "./ledger";

type Props = {
  state: LedgerState;
  amountCents?: number; // optional
  compact?: boolean;
  leftLabel?: string;   // "Client"
  rightLabel?: string;  // "Cleaner"
};

function formatMoney(amountCents?: number) {
  if (amountCents == null) return null;
  const dollars = amountCents / 100;
  return dollars.toLocaleString(undefined, { style: "currency", currency: "USD" });
}

export default function LedgerFlow({
  state,
  amountCents,
  compact = false,
  leftLabel = "Client",
  rightLabel = "Cleaner",
}: Props) {
  const w = compact ? 360 : 520;
  const h = compact ? 92 : 110;

  const color = getLedgerColor(state);
  const statusText = getLedgerLabel(state);
  const amountText = formatMoney(amountCents);

  // Curved path across the rail
  const path = `M 50 ${h / 2} C ${w * 0.35} ${h * 0.15}, ${w * 0.65} ${h * 0.85}, ${w - 50} ${h / 2}`;

  // Particles only when moving
  const particleCount = compact ? 3 : 5;

  return (
    <div className="w-full">
      <div
        className="rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-white/5 p-4"
        style={{ maxWidth: w }}
      >
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
          <div className="text-xs text-white/70">{leftLabel}</div>

          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            {amountText && (
              <span className="text-xs font-medium text-white/85 tabular-nums">
                {amountText}
              </span>
            )}
            <span
              className="text-[11px] font-medium"
              style={{ color }}
            >
              {statusText}
            </span>
          </div>

          <div className="text-xs text-white/70">{rightLabel}</div>
        </div>

        <div className="mt-3">
          <svg width={w} height={h} viewBox={`0 0 ${w} ${h}`} className="block">
            {/* Endpoints */}
            <circle cx={50} cy={h / 2} r={compact ? 10 : 12} fill="rgba(255,255,255,0.92)" />
            <circle cx={w - 50} cy={h / 2} r={compact ? 10 : 12} fill="rgba(255,255,255,0.92)" />

            {/* Soft endpoint glow when settled */}
            {state === "settled" && (
              <>
                <circle cx={w - 50} cy={h / 2} r={compact ? 18 : 22} fill="rgba(34,197,94,0.10)" />
                <circle cx={w - 50} cy={h / 2} r={compact ? 28 : 34} fill="rgba(34,197,94,0.06)" />
              </>
            )}

            {/* Track */}
            <path
              d={path}
              fill="none"
              stroke="rgba(255,255,255,0.12)"
              strokeWidth={compact ? 3 : 4}
              strokeLinecap="round"
            />

            {/* Active rail overlay */}
            <motion.path
              d={path}
              fill="none"
              stroke={color}
              strokeWidth={compact ? 3 : 4}
              strokeLinecap="round"
              initial={false}
              animate={{
                pathLength: state === "pending" ? 0.1 : state === "moving" ? 0.7 : 1,
                opacity: state === "pending" ? 0.55 : 0.95,
              }}
              transition={{ duration: 0.7, ease: "easeInOut" }}
              style={{
                filter:
                  state === "moving"
                    ? "drop-shadow(0px 0px 10px rgba(96,165,250,0.18))"
                    : state === "settled"
                    ? "drop-shadow(0px 0px 10px rgba(34,197,94,0.18))"
                    : "none",
              }}
            />

            {/* Particles moving along the path */}
            {state === "moving" &&
              Array.from({ length: particleCount }).map((_, i) => {
                const delay = i * 0.25;
                const radius = compact ? 3 : 3.5;

                return (
                  <motion.circle
                    key={i}
                    r={radius}
                    fill={color}
                    initial={false}
                    animate={{
                      offsetDistance: ["0%", "100%"],
                      opacity: [0, 1, 1, 0],
                      scale: [0.9, 1.0, 1.0, 0.9],
                    }}
                    transition={{
                      duration: 1.6,
                      ease: "linear",
                      repeat: Infinity,
                      delay,
                    }}
                    style={
                      {
                        offsetPath: `path("${path}")`,
                        offsetDistance: "0%",
                      } as any
                    }
                  />
                );
              })}
          </svg>
        </div>

        {/* Optional explanatory microcopy */}
        <div className="mt-2 text-[11px] text-white/60">
          {state === "pending" && "Funds are held until the task starts."}
          {state === "moving" && "Credits are transferring securely."}
          {state === "settled" && "Transfer complete — ledger updated."}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
Note: This uses CSS offset-path, which is supported in modern Chromium/Edge/Safari. If you need rock-solid fallback for older browsers, I’ll give you the JS getPointAtLength() version next.

Alright 😈✅ #3 Map + Presence System — starting with 3A: Presence Overlay (approach dot → arrival pulse → check-in perimeter glow).

We’re going to build this provider-agnostic first (works on top of Mapbox, Google Maps, or even a plain div), then you’ll drop it onto the actual map container.

This is 2D (SVG + Framer Motion) so it’s fast and clean.

3️⃣A — Presence Overlay Components
What you’ll have after this step
ApproachDotOverlay — animates a dot moving along a route toward the home

ArrivalPulse — pulses at the destination when “arrived”

CheckInPerimeter — draws a subtle ring around the home when checked-in

The only requirement: you supply pixel coordinates of the route and destination relative to the map container.

Folder structure
Create:

/components/presence
  PresenceOverlay.tsx
  presenceMath.ts
File 1: components/presence/presenceMath.ts
Utilities for route interpolation + pixel-space motion.

export type Point = { x: number; y: number };

export function lerp(a: number, b: number, t: number) {
  return a + (b - a) * t;
}

export function clamp01(t: number) {
  return Math.max(0, Math.min(1, t));
}

export function dist(a: Point, b: Point) {
  const dx = b.x - a.x;
  const dy = b.y - a.y;
  return Math.hypot(dx, dy);
}

export function polylineLength(points: Point[]) {
  let total = 0;
  for (let i = 1; i < points.length; i++) total += dist(points[i - 1], points[i]);
  return total;
}

// Returns point at normalized progress [0..1] along polyline
export function pointOnPolyline(points: Point[], t01: number): Point {
  if (points.length === 0) return { x: 0, y: 0 };
  if (points.length === 1) return points[0];

  const t = clamp01(t01);
  const total = polylineLength(points);
  if (total <= 0) return points[0];

  let target = total * t;
  for (let i = 1; i < points.length; i++) {
    const a = points[i - 1];
    const b = points[i];
    const seg = dist(a, b);
    if (target <= seg) {
      const localT = seg === 0 ? 0 : target / seg;
      return { x: lerp(a.x, b.x, localT), y: lerp(a.y, b.y, localT) };
    }
    target -= seg;
  }
  return points[points.length - 1];
}

// SVG path string for polyline (for optional route rendering)
export function svgPath(points: Point[]) {
  if (!points.length) return "";
  return points
    .map((p, i) => `${i === 0 ? "M" : "L"} ${p.x.toFixed(2)} ${p.y.toFixed(2)}`)
    .join(" ");
}
File 2: components/presence/PresenceOverlay.tsx
This renders the three effects. It expects pixel-space inputs.

"use client";

import { motion } from "framer-motion";
import { Point, pointOnPolyline, svgPath } from "./presenceMath";
import { useMemo } from "react";

type Props = {
  width: number;              // map container width (px)
  height: number;             // map container height (px)

  // Route in PIXELS relative to the container (top-left = 0,0)
  routePx?: Point[];

  // Destination in PIXELS
  destinationPx: Point;

  // 0..1 progress along the route (if routePx provided)
  progress?: number;

  // States
  arrived?: boolean;          // triggers arrival pulse
  checkedIn?: boolean;        // triggers perimeter ring
  showRoute?: boolean;        // optional debug/visual
};

export default function PresenceOverlay({
  width,
  height,
  routePx,
  destinationPx,
  progress = 0,
  arrived = false,
  checkedIn = false,
  showRoute = false,
}: Props) {
  const dot = useMemo(() => {
    if (!routePx || routePx.length < 2) return destinationPx;
    return pointOnPolyline(routePx, progress);
  }, [routePx, progress, destinationPx]);

  const routePath = useMemo(() => (routePx ? svgPath(routePx) : ""), [routePx]);

  return (
    <div className="pointer-events-none absolute inset-0">
      <svg width={width} height={height} viewBox={`0 0 ${width} ${height}`} className="block">
        {/* Optional route rendering (subtle) */}
        {showRoute && routePx && routePx.length >= 2 && (
          <>
            <path
              d={routePath}
              fill="none"
              stroke="rgba(255,255,255,0.10)"
              strokeWidth={3}
              strokeLinecap="round"
            />
            <path
              d={routePath}
              fill="none"
              stroke="rgba(96,165,250,0.35)"
              strokeWidth={3}
              strokeLinecap="round"
              strokeDasharray="6 10"
            />
          </>
        )}

        {/* Check-in perimeter glow around destination */}
        {checkedIn && (
          <>
            <motion.circle
              cx={destinationPx.x}
              cy={destinationPx.y}
              r={38}
              fill="rgba(34,197,94,0.08)"
              animate={{ opacity: [0.18, 0.32, 0.18], r: [34, 42, 34] }}
              transition={{ duration: 2.0, repeat: Infinity, ease: "easeInOut" }}
            />
            <circle
              cx={destinationPx.x}
              cy={destinationPx.y}
              r={48}
              fill="none"
              stroke="rgba(34,197,94,0.25)"
              strokeWidth={1.5}
            />
          </>
        )}

        {/* Arrival pulse (one or looping) */}
        {arrived && (
          <motion.circle
            cx={destinationPx.x}
            cy={destinationPx.y}
            r={16}
            fill="none"
            stroke="rgba(34,197,94,0.45)"
            strokeWidth={2}
            animate={{ opacity: [0.0, 0.7, 0.0], r: [14, 58, 14] }}
            transition={{ duration: 1.8, repeat: Infinity, ease: "easeInOut" }}
          />
        )}

        {/* Moving approach dot */}
        <motion.g
          initial={false}
          animate={{ x: dot.x, y: dot.y }}
          transition={{ duration: 0.25, ease: "easeOut" }}
        >
          {/* Outer soft glow */}
          <circle cx={0} cy={0} r={10} fill="rgba(96,165,250,0.14)" />
          <circle cx={0} cy={0} r={16} fill="rgba(96,165,250,0.08)" />

          {/* Core dot */}
          <circle cx={0} cy={0} r={5.5} fill="rgba(255,255,255,0.92)" />
          <circle cx={0} cy={0} r={5.5} fill="rgba(96,165,250,0.35)" />
        </motion.g>

        {/* Destination marker (subtle anchor) */}
        <circle cx={destinationPx.x} cy={destinationPx.y} r={6} fill="rgba(255,255,255,0.55)" />
      </svg>
    </div>
  );
}
3️⃣A Demo Harness (so you can see it working immediately)
Create a simple “fake map” container and animate progress.

File 3: components/presence/PresenceDemo.tsx
"use client";

import { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from "react";
import PresenceOverlay from "./PresenceOverlay";
import type { Point } from "./presenceMath";

export default function PresenceDemo() {
  const width = 820;
  const height = 420;

  // Example pixel route (pretend this came from map projection)
  const routePx: Point[] = useMemo(
    () => [
      { x: 80, y: 320 },
      { x: 180, y: 260 },
      { x: 320, y: 270 },
      { x: 460, y: 190 },
      { x: 610, y: 210 },
      { x: 730, y: 140 },
    ],
    []
  );

  const destinationPx = routePx[routePx.length - 1];

  const [progress, setProgress] = useState(0);
  const [arrived, setArrived] = useState(false);
  const [checkedIn, setCheckedIn] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    const t = setInterval(() => {
      setProgress((p) => {
        const next = Math.min(1, p + 0.01);
        if (next >= 1) {
          setArrived(true);
          // simulate check-in shortly after arrival
          setTimeout(() => setCheckedIn(true), 900);
        }
        return next;
      });
    }, 60);
    return () => clearInterval(t);
  }, []);

  return (
    <div className="rounded-3xl border border-white/10 bg-[#0B0E14] p-6">
      <div className="mb-3 text-sm font-semibold text-white">Map + Presence Overlay (Demo)</div>

      <div
        className="relative overflow-hidden rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-white/5"
        style={{ width, height }}
      >
        {/* Fake map background */}
        <div className="absolute inset-0 opacity-70" style={{
          background:
            "radial-gradient(800px 320px at 30% 40%, rgba(96,165,250,0.10), transparent 60%), radial-gradient(700px 280px at 70% 55%, rgba(34,197,94,0.10), transparent 60%)"
        }} />

        {/* Presence overlay */}
        <PresenceOverlay
          width={width}
          height={height}
          routePx={routePx}
          destinationPx={destinationPx}
          progress={progress}
          arrived={arrived}
          checkedIn={checkedIn}
          showRoute={true}
        />

        {/* HUD */}
        <div className="absolute left-4 top-4 rounded-xl border border-white/10 bg-black/35 px-3 py-2 text-xs text-white/75 backdrop-blur">
          progress: {Math.round(progress * 100)}%
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

  return (
    <main className="min-h-screen bg-[#0B0E14] p-8 text-white">

    </main>
  );

Here’s what I’d do.

What this means (current state)
✅ You are not using Google Maps SDK (no embedded map, no API key usage)

✅ Backend only generates a Google Maps Directions URL and punts to the Google Maps app/site

✅ Lat/lng exist in your DB and you do approx distance math in code

✅ You have no geocoding pipeline (address → lat/lng) and no “real route distance/time” yet

This is a perfectly normal early-stage state.

What you should do next (best path)
Phase 1 — Keep “Get directions” link (don’t break ops)
Do nothing to backend for this part. The link is good.

Reason: it’s reliable, free, and works on every device.

Phase 2 — Add the Map + Presence system in the FRONTEND only (progressive enhancement)

Option A (Recommended): Add Google Maps JS SDK in the frontend (only where needed)
You keep backend the same.

Frontend gets:

embedded map

ability to project lat/lng → pixel coordinates

your PresenceOverlay becomes real (approach dot + arrival pulse + check-in ring)

Why this is best: your PresenceOverlay needs pixel mapping. Google Maps JS gives you projection.

What changes:

Add a Google Maps API key (frontend env var)

One new “tracking page” map component

Option B (Cheapest): No embedded map; use a branded “tracking canvas”
If you don’t want API keys yet:

show a stylized “map-like” background panel (not a real map)

show your Presence overlay on top

still keep “Open in Google Maps” for actual navigation

Why: still feels “alive” without needing SDK, but it’s not a true map.

1) Add a key safely

Use OverlayView methods to convert lat/lng → container pixels

Then feed those pixel points into the PresenceOverlay we built.

Result:

real map tiles from Google

your approach dot moves correctly on top

For the approach dot:

you can start with a straight-line interpolation from cleaner → home

later replace with real route polyline if/when you add Directions API

This keeps costs near-zero early.

Right now you do rough distance math. That’s fine early.

When you want production-grade matching and ETA, upgrade in this order:

lat, lng

normalized address

Instead of haversine distance:

Cache results (very important) so you don’t pay repeatedly

Only needed if you want the dot to follow roads.

Directions API / Routes API

decode polyline, project to pixels, feed to overlay

does this follow best practices?

Mostly yes ✅ — for an MVP / early-stage marketplace, your current setup is aligned with best practices given the goal is “don’t add cost/complexity until you need it.” But it’s not best practice for production-grade mapping, ETAs, and matching accuracy yet.

Here’s the precise assessment.

What you’re doing now
1) “Get directions” = Google Maps URL link
✅ Best practice for MVP.
Deep-linking to Google Maps is:

reliable across devices

requires no SDK

requires no API key

avoids expensive routing APIs

avoids map rendering performance risks

This is a common pattern even in mature products (they often keep “Open in Maps” as the canonical nav path).

2) No Map SDK, no map rendering
✅ Also fine if you don’t need in-app tracking right now.

3) Matching uses stored lat/lng + simple distance math
✅ Best practice for stage-0 matching (shortlist quickly, no external dependency).
But it becomes ❌ later if it drives ETAs, pricing, or “guaranteed arrival windows.”

Where it falls short of “production best practices”
These are the gaps you’ll eventually need to address:

A) No geocoding pipeline
If users enter addresses, you need a trustworthy address → lat/lng process.

Without it, you risk wrong coordinates, bad matching, failed arrivals.

Best practice: geocode once at job creation, store lat/lng + optionally place_id.

B) Haversine ≠ travel time
Distance-as-the-crow-flies can be badly wrong in:

cities (one-way streets)

water / bridges

highways

mountainous areas

Best practice: use haversine to shortlist, then route/ETA API for top candidates.

C) No caching strategy (for when you add routing)
When you do add Distance Matrix / Routes:

calling it on every search will blow up cost + latency

Best practice: cache route results keyed by origin grid + destination grid + time bucket.

D) Privacy / safety posture (if you do live presence later)
If you add live tracking:

raw GPS at high frequency creates privacy and liability concerns

Best practice:

minimize precision shown to customers (e.g., “within ~200m” until arrival)

store only what you need, with retention limits

audit trail and explicit consent

E) Vendor strategy
Right now your “integration” is a link, so vendor risk is low.
But once you embed maps:

you’ll want consistent provider usage + fallback plan

Best practice: abstract map provider behind a small interface (frontend) so you can switch later.

Best-practice recommendation for PureTask (what to do)
Keep current approach as the baseline ✅
Keep the Google directions link exactly as-is

It’s a best-practice fallback forever

Add “in-app presence” only when you need it, and do it cleanly ✅
When ready, best practice is:

Phase 1 (low cost, clean)
Frontend: embed Google Maps JS SDK only on tracking pages

Use your 2D PresenceOverlay on top

Route motion: simple interpolation cleaner→home (good enough)

Phase 2 (accuracy upgrade)
Add geocoding at job creation

Add Distance Matrix / Routes for ETA (only for top N matches)

Cache results

Phase 3 (premium)
Directions polyline for “dot follows roads”

Better UI states (arrived, checked-in, started, completed)

Quick “best practice scorecard”
MVP best practices: ✅✅✅✅ (strong)
Production mapping best practices: ✅✅ (needs upgrades when you embed maps / promise ETAs)

If you want the cleanest “best practice” next step
Do not add Mapbox just because docs mention it.

Instead:

Keep Google link as fallback

If you embed maps later, use Google Maps JS SDK since you’re already in the Google ecosystem

Build a tiny frontend abstraction so you’re not locked in

If you tell me whether you want customer tracking or cleaner on-route first, I’ll give you the best-practice implementation plan for that page (including provider abstraction + privacy defaults). 😈

# Data Model Reference: Job, Cleaner, Payment

Single reference for DB schemas, TypeScript types, API response shapes, and retrieval queries for Job details and related entities.

---

## A) DB schemas / SQL table definitions

There is **no Prisma** in this repo; the app uses raw SQL and src/db/client (e.g. query()). Tables are created in DB/migrations/ (e.g. 000_COMPLETE_CONSOLIDATED_SCHEMA.sql, 001_init.sql).

### Enums (used by tables below)

sql
CREATE TYPE user_role AS ENUM ('client', 'cleaner', 'admin');
CREATE TYPE job_status AS ENUM (
  'requested', 'accepted', 'on_my_way', 'in_progress',
  'awaiting_approval', 'completed', 'disputed', 'cancelled'
);
CREATE TYPE credit_reason AS ENUM (
  'purchase', 'wallet_topup', 'job_escrow', 'job_release', 'refund', 'adjustment'
);
CREATE TYPE payout_status AS ENUM ('pending', 'paid', 'failed');
CREATE TYPE dispute_status AS ENUM ('open', 'resolved_refund', 'resolved_no_refund');


### Users (base for Client/Cleaner)

sql
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
  id              TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid()::TEXT,
  email           CITEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
  password_hash   TEXT NOT NULL,
  role            user_role NOT NULL DEFAULT 'client',
  first_name      TEXT,
  last_name       TEXT,
  phone           TEXT,
  referral_code   TEXT UNIQUE,
  created_at      TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at      TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
);


(Additional columns exist in consolidated schema: email_verified, password_reset_*, two_factor_*, last_login_at, etc.)

### Cleaner (users + cleaner_profiles)

sql
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS cleaner_profiles (
  id                       UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  user_id                  TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE REFERENCES users (id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  first_name               TEXT,
  last_name                TEXT,
  bio                      TEXT,
  tier                     TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'bronze',
  reliability_score        NUMERIC(5,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 100.0,
  reliability_last_computed TIMESTAMPTZ,
  hourly_rate_credits      INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  base_rate_cph            NUMERIC(10,2),
  deep_addon_cph           NUMERIC(10,2),
  moveout_addon_cph        NUMERIC(10,2),
  avg_rating               NUMERIC(3,2),
  jobs_completed           INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  low_flexibility_badge    BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT false,
  payout_percent           NUMERIC(5,2) DEFAULT 80,
  stripe_connect_id        TEXT,
  stripe_account_id        TEXT,
  latitude                 NUMERIC(9,6),
  longitude                NUMERIC(9,6),
  is_available             BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
  travel_radius_km         NUMERIC(5,2) DEFAULT 50,
  max_jobs_per_day         INTEGER DEFAULT 5,
  accepts_high_risk        BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  minimum_payout_cents      INTEGER DEFAULT 2500,
  payout_schedule          TEXT DEFAULT 'weekly',
  instant_payout_enabled   BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  background_check_required BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
  background_check_status   TEXT DEFAULT 'not_started',
  push_token               TEXT,
  onboarding_current_step  TEXT DEFAULT 'terms',
  onboarding_reminder_sent_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  onboarding_started_at     TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),
  onboarding_completed_at   TIMESTAMPTZ,
  created_at               TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at               TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
);
-- avatar_url may be added in later migrations


### Job

sql
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS jobs (
  id                      UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  client_id               TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES users (id) ON DELETE RESTRICT,
  cleaner_id              TEXT REFERENCES users (id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  property_id             INT REFERENCES properties(id),
  address_id              UUID REFERENCES addresses(id),
  team_id                 INT REFERENCES cleaner_teams(id),
  status                  job_status NOT NULL DEFAULT 'requested',
  scheduled_start_at      TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
  scheduled_end_at        TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
  actual_start_at         TIMESTAMPTZ,
  actual_end_at           TIMESTAMPTZ,
  address                 TEXT NOT NULL,
  latitude                NUMERIC(9,6),
  longitude               NUMERIC(9,6),
  credit_amount           INTEGER NOT NULL,
  cleaning_type           TEXT,
  duration_hours          NUMERIC(4,2),
  price_credits           INTEGER,
  held_credits            INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  rating                  INTEGER CHECK (rating BETWEEN 1 AND 5),
  client_notes            TEXT,
  notes_client            TEXT,
  notes_cleaner           TEXT,
  cleaner_payout_amount_cents INTEGER,
  is_rush                 BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  rush_fee_credits        INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  created_at              TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at              TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
);


### Payment / credits

**Credit ledger** (source of truth for credit movements; job-related entries have job_id set):

sql
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS credit_ledger (
  id              UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  user_id         TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES users (id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  job_id          UUID REFERENCES jobs (id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  delta_credits   INTEGER NOT NULL,
  reason          credit_reason NOT NULL,
  created_at      TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
);


**Payment intents** (Stripe; job charge or wallet top-up):

sql
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS payment_intents (
  id                          UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  job_id                      UUID REFERENCES jobs (id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  client_id                   TEXT REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  stripe_payment_intent_id    TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
  status                      TEXT NOT NULL,
  amount_cents                INTEGER NOT NULL,
  currency                    TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'usd',
  purpose                     TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'wallet_topup',  -- 'wallet_topup' | 'job_charge'
  credits_amount              INTEGER,
  created_at                  TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at                  TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
);


**Payouts** (cleaner earnings paid out):

sql
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS payouts (
  id                  UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  cleaner_id          TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES users (id) ON DELETE RESTRICT,
  job_id             UUID REFERENCES jobs(id),
  stripe_transfer_id  TEXT,
  amount_credits     INTEGER NOT NULL,
  amount_cents       INTEGER NOT NULL,
  total_usd          NUMERIC(10,2),
  status             payout_status NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending',
  created_at         TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at         TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
);

## B) TypeScript types / interfaces

### From src/types/db.ts (canonical for DB rows)

ts
// Job (matches jobs table)
export type JobStatus =
  | "requested" | "accepted" | "on_my_way" | "in_progress"
  | "awaiting_approval" | "completed" | "disputed" | "cancelled";

export interface Job {
  id: string;
  client_id: string;
  cleaner_id: string | null;
  address_id: string | null;
  status: JobStatus;
  scheduled_start_at: string;
  scheduled_end_at: string;
  actual_start_at: string | null;
  actual_end_at: string | null;
  address: string;
  latitude: number | null;
  longitude: number | null;
  credit_amount: number;
  cleaning_type: CleaningType | null;  // "basic" | "deep" | "move_out" | "recurring"
  duration_hours: number | null;
  price_credits: number | null;

## C) API responses (example JSON)

### GET /jobs/:jobId

**Response:** 200 OK  
**Wrapper:** sendSuccess(res, { job }) → body is { data: { job } }.

json
{
  "data": {
    "job": {
      "id": "uuid",
      "client_id": "user-id",
      "cleaner_id": "user-id-or-null",
      "address_id": null,
      "status": "requested",
      "scheduled_start_at": "2025-02-10T09:00:00.000Z",
      "scheduled_end_at": "2025-02-10T11:00:00.000Z",
      "actual_start_at": null,
      "actual_end_at": null,
      "address": "123 Main St, City, ST 12345",
      "latitude": 37.7749,
      "longitude": -122.4194,
      "credit_amount": 100,
      "cleaning_type": "basic",
      "duration_hours": 2,
      "price_credits": 100,
      "held_credits": 0,
      "cleaner_payout_amount_cents": null,
      "rating": null,
      "client_notes": null,
      "notes_cleaner": null,
      "created_at": "2025-02-09T12:00:00.000Z",
      "updated_at": "2025-02-09T12:00:00.000Z"
    }
  }
}


404: { "error": { "code": "NOT_FOUND", "message": "Job not found" } }.  
403: forbidden if not client/cleaner/admin for that job.

---

### GET /cleaners/:id

**Response:** 200 OK  
**Body:** { cleaner } (no data wrapper in dashboardStubs; other routers may use data).

json
{
  "cleaner": {
    "id": "user-uuid",
    "email": "cleaner@example.com",
    "name": "Jane Doe",
    "avatar_url": null,
    "bio": "Professional cleaner.",
    "base_rate_cph": 25.00,
    "level": 3,
    "badges": [
      { "id": "badge-uuid", "name": "On Time", "icon": "clock" }
    ]
  }
}


404: { "error": { "code": "NOT_FOUND", "message": "Cleaner not found" } }.

---

### GET /payments/history

**Query:** ?purpose=wallet_topup|job_charge&limit=50  
**Response:** list of payment intents for current user; each item can have jobId.

json
{
  "payments": [
    {
      "id": "pi-uuid",
      "purpose": "job_charge",
      "status": "succeeded",
      "amountCents": 5000,
      "amountFormatted": "$50.00",
      "credits": 100,
      "jobId": "job-uuid",
      "createdAt": "2025-02-09T12:00:00.000Z"
    }
  ],
  "count": 1
}


There is **no** dedicated GET /payments?jobId=... endpoint. To get “payment/ledger for a job” use the service/query below.

---

### POST /payments/job/:jobId (create job charge)

**Response:** payment intent + pricing breakdown.

json
{
  "clientSecret": "pi_xxx_secret_xxx",
  "paymentIntentId": "pi_xxx",
  "jobId": "job-uuid",
  "credits": 100,
  "baseAmountCents": 5000,
  "surchargePercent": 5,
  "surchargeAmountCents": 250,
  "totalAmountCents": 5250,
  "totalAmountFormatted": "$52.50",
  "pricingNote": "Includes 5% convenience fee. Use wallet credits to save!"
}


---

### GET /payments/balance

json
{
  "balance": 250,
  "balanceFormatted": "250 credits",
  "valueInCents": 12500,
  "valueFormatted": "$125.00"
}


---

## D) Exact retrieval queries for “Job details” page

Conceptually, to power a Job details page you need:

1. **Job by id**  
   - **Query:** SELECT * FROM jobs WHERE id = $1  
   - **Service:** getJob(jobId) or getJobById(jobId) in src/services/jobsService.ts.

2. **Cleaner by job.cleaner_id**  
   - **Query:**  
     - User: SELECT * FROM users WHERE id = $1  
     - Profile: SELECT * FROM cleaner_profiles WHERE user_id = $1  
   - **API:** GET /cleaners/:id (id = job.cleaner_id) returns combined profile + level + badges.  
   - **Service:** no single “getCleaner(cleanerId)” in one place; dashboardStubs does ad‑hoc query + level + badges.

3. **Payment / ledger by job.id**  
   - **Credit ledger entries for job:**  
     - **Query:** SELECT * FROM credit_ledger WHERE job_id = $1 ORDER BY created_at ASC  
     - **Service:** getJobCreditEntries(jobId) in src/services/creditsService.ts.  
   - **Payment intents for job:**  
     - **Query:** SELECT * FROM payment_intents WHERE job_id = $1 AND purpose = 'job_charge'  
     - **Stripe:** GET /stripe/payment-intent/:jobId (in src/routes/stripe.ts) returns payment intent for that job.

4. **Cleaner last location (optional)**  
   - **Source:** jobs has latitude, longitude for the **job address**.  
   - **Cleaner’s current location** is not in a separate “last_location” table in the main schema; it may come from:  
     - Check-in/tracking events (e.g. job_events or tracking payload with lat/lng), or  
     - cleaner_profiles.latitude / cleaner_profiles.longitude (home/base), not live GPS.  
   - So “cleaner last location” for a given job would be: either the latest check-in/tracking event for that job (if stored), or N/A if only base location is stored.

### Summary: queries to run for Job details page

| Data            | Query / service / endpoint |
|-----------------|----------------------------|
| Job by id       | SELECT * FROM jobs WHERE id = $1 or getJob(jobId) |
| Cleaner         | GET /cleaners/:id with id = job.cleaner_id, or join users + cleaner_profiles on user_id = job.cleaner_id |
| Ledger for job  | SELECT * FROM credit_ledger WHERE job_id = $1 ORDER BY created_at ASC or getJobCreditEntries(jobId) |
| Payment for job | SELECT * FROM payment_intents WHERE job_id = $1 and/or GET /stripe/payment-intent/:jobId |
| Cleaner location| Job address: jobs.latitude, jobs.longitude. Live cleaner location: from tracking/check-in events if persisted; otherwise cleaner_profiles.latitude/longitude (base). |

---

  is_reasonable: boolean;
  created_at: string;
  updated_at: string;
}

# Data Model Reference: Job, Cleaner, Payment

Single reference for DB schemas, TypeScript types, API response shapes, and retrieval queries for Job details and related entities.

---

## A) DB schemas / SQL table definitions

There is **no Prisma** in this repo; the app uses raw SQL and src/db/client (e.g. query()). Tables are created in DB/migrations/ (e.g. 000_COMPLETE_CONSOLIDATED_SCHEMA.sql, 001_init.sql).

### Enums (used by tables below)

sql
CREATE TYPE user_role AS ENUM ('client', 'cleaner', 'admin');
CREATE TYPE job_status AS ENUM (
  'requested', 'accepted', 'on_my_way', 'in_progress',
  'awaiting_approval', 'completed', 'disputed', 'cancelled'
);
CREATE TYPE credit_reason AS ENUM (
  'purchase', 'wallet_topup', 'job_escrow', 'job_release', 'refund', 'adjustment'
);
CREATE TYPE payout_status AS ENUM ('pending', 'paid', 'failed');
CREATE TYPE dispute_status AS ENUM ('open', 'resolved_refund', 'resolved_no_refund');


### Users (base for Client/Cleaner)

sql
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
  id              TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid()::TEXT,
  email           CITEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
  password_hash   TEXT NOT NULL,
  role            user_role NOT NULL DEFAULT 'client',
  first_name      TEXT,
  last_name       TEXT,
  phone           TEXT,
  referral_code   TEXT UNIQUE,
  created_at      TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at      TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
);


(Additional columns exist in consolidated schema: email_verified, password_reset_*, two_factor_*, last_login_at, etc.)

### Cleaner (users + cleaner_profiles)

sql
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS cleaner_profiles (
  id                       UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  user_id                  TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE REFERENCES users (id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  first_name               TEXT,
  last_name                TEXT,
  bio                      TEXT,
  tier                     TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'bronze',
  reliability_score        NUMERIC(5,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 100.0,
  reliability_last_computed TIMESTAMPTZ,
  hourly_rate_credits      INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  base_rate_cph            NUMERIC(10,2),
  deep_addon_cph           NUMERIC(10,2),
  moveout_addon_cph        NUMERIC(10,2),
  avg_rating               NUMERIC(3,2),
  jobs_completed           INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  low_flexibility_badge    BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT false,
  payout_percent           NUMERIC(5,2) DEFAULT 80,
  stripe_connect_id        TEXT,
  stripe_account_id        TEXT,
  latitude                 NUMERIC(9,6),
  longitude                NUMERIC(9,6),
  is_available             BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
  travel_radius_km         NUMERIC(5,2) DEFAULT 50,
  max_jobs_per_day         INTEGER DEFAULT 5,
  accepts_high_risk        BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  minimum_payout_cents      INTEGER DEFAULT 2500,
  payout_schedule          TEXT DEFAULT 'weekly',
  instant_payout_enabled   BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  background_check_required BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
  background_check_status   TEXT DEFAULT 'not_started',
  push_token               TEXT,
  onboarding_current_step  TEXT DEFAULT 'terms',
  onboarding_reminder_sent_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  onboarding_started_at     TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),
  onboarding_completed_at   TIMESTAMPTZ,
  created_at               TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at               TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
);
-- avatar_url may be added in later migrations


### Job

sql
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS jobs (
  id                      UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  client_id               TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES users (id) ON DELETE RESTRICT,
  cleaner_id              TEXT REFERENCES users (id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  property_id             INT REFERENCES properties(id),
  address_id              UUID REFERENCES addresses(id),
  team_id                 INT REFERENCES cleaner_teams(id),
  status                  job_status NOT NULL DEFAULT 'requested',
  scheduled_start_at      TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
  scheduled_end_at        TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
  actual_start_at         TIMESTAMPTZ,
  actual_end_at           TIMESTAMPTZ,
  address                 TEXT NOT NULL,
  latitude                NUMERIC(9,6),
  longitude               NUMERIC(9,6),
  credit_amount           INTEGER NOT NULL,
  cleaning_type           TEXT,
  duration_hours          NUMERIC(4,2),
  price_credits           INTEGER,
  held_credits            INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  rating                  INTEGER CHECK (rating BETWEEN 1 AND 5),
  client_notes            TEXT,
  notes_client            TEXT,
  notes_cleaner           TEXT,
  cleaner_payout_amount_cents INTEGER,
  is_rush                 BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  rush_fee_credits        INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  created_at              TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at              TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
);


### Payment / credits

**Credit ledger** (source of truth for credit movements; job-related entries have job_id set):

sql
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS credit_ledger (
  id              UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  user_id         TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES users (id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  job_id          UUID REFERENCES jobs (id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  delta_credits   INTEGER NOT NULL,
  reason          credit_reason NOT NULL,
  created_at      TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
);


**Payment intents** (Stripe; job charge or wallet top-up):

sql
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS payment_intents (
  id                          UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  job_id                      UUID REFERENCES jobs (id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  client_id                   TEXT REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  stripe_payment_intent_id    TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
  status                      TEXT NOT NULL,
  amount_cents                INTEGER NOT NULL,
  currency                    TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'usd',
  purpose                     TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'wallet_topup',  -- 'wallet_topup' | 'job_charge'
  credits_amount              INTEGER,
  created_at                  TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at                  TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
);


**Payouts** (cleaner earnings paid out):

sql
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS payouts (
  id                  UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  cleaner_id          TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES users (id) ON DELETE RESTRICT,
  job_id             UUID REFERENCES jobs(id),
  stripe_transfer_id  TEXT,
  amount_credits     INTEGER NOT NULL,
  amount_cents       INTEGER NOT NULL,
  total_usd          NUMERIC(10,2),
  status             payout_status NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending',
  created_at         TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at         TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
);

## B) TypeScript types / interfaces

### From src/types/db.ts (canonical for DB rows)

ts
// Job (matches jobs table)
export type JobStatus =
  | "requested" | "accepted" | "on_my_way" | "in_progress"
  | "awaiting_approval" | "completed" | "disputed" | "cancelled";

export interface Job {
  id: string;
  client_id: string;
  cleaner_id: string | null;
  address_id: string | null;
  status: JobStatus;
  scheduled_start_at: string;
  scheduled_end_at: string;
  actual_start_at: string | null;
  actual_end_at: string | null;
  address: string;
  latitude: number | null;
  longitude: number | null;
  credit_amount: number;
  cleaning_type: CleaningType | null;  // "basic" | "deep" | "move_out" | "recurring"
  duration_hours: number | null;
  price_credits: number | null;
  held_credits: number;
  cleaner_payout_amount_cents: number | null;
  rating: number | null;
  client_notes: string | null;
  notes_cleaner: string | null;
  created_at: string;
  updated_at: string;
}

// Cleaner profile (matches cleaner_profiles table)
export interface CleanerProfile {
  id: string;
  user_id: string;
  first_name: string | null;
  last_name: string | null;
  bio: string | null;
  tier: string;
  reliability_score: number;
  hourly_rate_credits: number;
  base_rate_cph: number | null;
  deep_addon_cph: number | null;
  moveout_addon_cph: number | null;
  avg_rating: number | null;
  jobs_completed: number;
  latitude: number | null;
  longitude: number | null;
  is_available: boolean;
  travel_radius_km: number | null;
  stripe_connect_id: string | null;
  stripe_account_id: string | null;
  created_at: string;
  updated_at: string;
  // ... more fields
}

// Credit ledger entry
export type CreditReason =
  | "purchase" | "subscription_credit" | "job_escrow" | "job_release"
  | "refund" | "adjustment" | "invoice_payment";

export interface CreditLedgerEntry {
  id: string;
  user_id: string;
  job_id: string | null;
  delta_credits: number;
  reason: CreditReason;
  created_at: string;
}

// Payment intent
export interface PaymentIntent {
  id: string;
  job_id: string | null;
  client_id: string | null;
  stripe_payment_intent_id: string;
  status: string;
  amount_cents: number;
  currency: string;
  purpose: "wallet_topup" | "job_charge";
  credits_amount: number | null;
  created_at: string;
  updated_at: string;
}

// Payout
export interface Payout {
  id: string;
  cleaner_id: string;
  job_id: string;
  stripe_transfer_id: string | null;
  amount_credits: number;
  amount_cents: number;
  total_usd: number;
  status: PayoutStatus;
  created_at: string;
  updated_at: string;
}


### From src/core/types.ts (core domain; some use numeric ids)

ts
export interface Job {
  id: number;
  clientId: number;
  cleanerId: number;
  startTime: Date;
  endTime: Date;
  heldCredits: number;
  status: string;
  address?: string;
  latitude?: number;
  longitude?: number;
}

export interface Cleaner {
  id: number;
  reliabilityScore: number;
  reliabilityTier: "Developing" | "Semi Pro" | "Pro" | "Elite";
  flexibilityStatus: "normal" | "low_flex";
  flexibilityBadgeActive: boolean;
}


### Other relevant types

- **User** (src/types/db.ts): id, email, role, first_name, last_name, etc.
- **JobWithDetails** (src/types/db.ts): extends Job with optional client_email, cleaner_email.
- **JobPhoto** (src/types/db.ts, src/services/photosService.ts): id, job_id, uploaded_by, type, url, etc.
- **CleanerEarning** (src/types/db.ts): cleaner_earnings table.

---

## C) API responses (example JSON)

### GET /jobs/:jobId

**Response:** 200 OK  
**Wrapper:** sendSuccess(res, { job }) → body is { data: { job } }.

json
{
  "data": {
    "job": {
      "id": "uuid",
      "client_id": "user-id",
      "cleaner_id": "user-id-or-null",
      "address_id": null,
      "status": "requested",
      "scheduled_start_at": "2025-02-10T09:00:00.000Z",
      "scheduled_end_at": "2025-02-10T11:00:00.000Z",
      "actual_start_at": null,
      "actual_end_at": null,
      "address": "123 Main St, City, ST 12345",
      "latitude": 37.7749,
      "longitude": -122.4194,
      "credit_amount": 100,
      "cleaning_type": "basic",
      "duration_hours": 2,
      "price_credits": 100,
      "held_credits": 0,
      "cleaner_payout_amount_cents": null,
      "rating": null,
      "client_notes": null,
      "notes_cleaner": null,
      "created_at": "2025-02-09T12:00:00.000Z",
      "updated_at": "2025-02-09T12:00:00.000Z"
    }
  }
}


404: { "error": { "code": "NOT_FOUND", "message": "Job not found" } }.  
403: forbidden if not client/cleaner/admin for that job.

---

### GET /cleaners/:id

**Response:** 200 OK  
**Body:** { cleaner } (no data wrapper in dashboardStubs; other routers may use data).

json
{
  "cleaner": {
    "id": "user-uuid",
    "email": "cleaner@example.com",
    "name": "Jane Doe",
    "avatar_url": null,
    "bio": "Professional cleaner.",
    "base_rate_cph": 25.00,
    "level": 3,
    "badges": [
      { "id": "badge-uuid", "name": "On Time", "icon": "clock" }
    ]
  }
}


404: { "error": { "code": "NOT_FOUND", "message": "Cleaner not found" } }.

---

### GET /payments/history

**Query:** ?purpose=wallet_topup|job_charge&limit=50  
**Response:** list of payment intents for current user; each item can have jobId.

json
{
  "payments": [
    {
      "id": "pi-uuid",
      "purpose": "job_charge",
      "status": "succeeded",
      "amountCents": 5000,
      "amountFormatted": "$50.00",
      "credits": 100,
      "jobId": "job-uuid",
      "createdAt": "2025-02-09T12:00:00.000Z"
    }
  ],
  "count": 1
}


There is **no** dedicated GET /payments?jobId=... endpoint. To get “payment/ledger for a job” use the service/query below.

---

### POST /payments/job/:jobId (create job charge)

**Response:** payment intent + pricing breakdown.

json
{
  "clientSecret": "pi_xxx_secret_xxx",
  "paymentIntentId": "pi_xxx",
  "jobId": "job-uuid",
  "credits": 100,
  "baseAmountCents": 5000,
  "surchargePercent": 5,
  "surchargeAmountCents": 250,
  "totalAmountCents": 5250,
  "totalAmountFormatted": "$52.50",
  "pricingNote": "Includes 5% convenience fee. Use wallet credits to save!"
}


---

### GET /payments/balance

json
{
  "balance": 250,
  "balanceFormatted": "250 credits",
  "valueInCents": 12500,
  "valueFormatted": "$125.00"
}

## D) Exact retrieval queries for “Job details” page

Conceptually, to power a Job details page you need:

1. **Job by id**  
   - **Query:** SELECT * FROM jobs WHERE id = $1  
   - **Service:** getJob(jobId) or getJobById(jobId) in src/services/jobsService.ts.

2. **Cleaner by job.cleaner_id**  
   - **Query:**  
     - User: SELECT * FROM users WHERE id = $1  
     - Profile: SELECT * FROM cleaner_profiles WHERE user_id = $1  
   - **API:** GET /cleaners/:id (id = job.cleaner_id) returns combined profile + level + badges.  
   - **Service:** no single “getCleaner(cleanerId)” in one place; dashboardStubs does ad‑hoc query + level + badges.

3. **Payment / ledger by job.id**  
   - **Credit ledger entries for job:**  
     - **Query:** SELECT * FROM credit_ledger WHERE job_id = $1 ORDER BY created_at ASC  
     - **Service:** getJobCreditEntries(jobId) in src/services/creditsService.ts.  
   - **Payment intents for job:**  
     - **Query:** SELECT * FROM payment_intents WHERE job_id = $1 AND purpose = 'job_charge'  
     - **Stripe:** GET /stripe/payment-intent/:jobId (in src/routes/stripe.ts) returns payment intent for that job.

4. **Cleaner last location (optional)**  
   - **Source:** jobs has latitude, longitude for the **job address**.  
   - **Cleaner’s current location** is not in a separate “last_location” table in the main schema; it may come from:  
     - Check-in/tracking events (e.g. job_events or tracking payload with lat/lng), or  
     - cleaner_profiles.latitude / cleaner_profiles.longitude (home/base), not live GPS.  
   - So “cleaner last location” for a given job would be: either the latest check-in/tracking event for that job (if stored), or N/A if only base location is stored.

### Summary: queries to run for Job details page

| Data            | Query / service / endpoint |
|-----------------|----------------------------|
| Job by id       | SELECT * FROM jobs WHERE id = $1 or getJob(jobId) |
| Cleaner         | GET /cleaners/:id with id = job.cleaner_id, or join users + cleaner_profiles on user_id = job.cleaner_id |
| Ledger for job  | SELECT * FROM credit_ledger WHERE job_id = $1 ORDER BY created_at ASC or getJobCreditEntries(jobId) |
| Payment for job | SELECT * FROM payment_intents WHERE job_id = $1 and/or GET /stripe/payment-intent/:jobId |
| Cleaner location| Job address: jobs.latitude, jobs.longitude. Live cleaner location: from tracking/check-in events if persisted; otherwise cleaner_profiles.latitude/longitude (base). |

---

## E) Frontend animation checklist — exact fields to retrieve

This section maps the “data audit” spec (Living Hero, Trust Visualization, Map + Presence, Interactive Cards, Task Builder) to PureTask’s current models and where to get each field. Use it to wire animations with **zero or minimal** backend changes.

### Status mapping (for Timeline Rail + Ledger Flow)

| Spec / UI value | PureTask field | Notes |
|-----------------|----------------|--------|
| **Job timeline** | | |
| booked | job.status = 'requested' or 'accepted' | Map both to “Booked” if you want one step. |
| on_route | job.status = 'on_my_way' | ✅ Direct. |
| working | job.status = 'in_progress' or 'awaiting_approval' | ✅ Direct. |
| completed | job.status = 'completed' | ✅ Direct. |
| cancelled | job.status = 'cancelled' | ✅ Direct. |
| pending_payment | No single status | Derive: job exists, no job_release ledger yet for that job. |
| **Ledger flow** | | |
| pending | Ledger: reason = 'job_escrow' (credits held) | ✅ Use credit_ledger entries for job. |
| moving | Ledger: reason = 'job_release' (credits released to cleaner) | ✅ Same. |
| settled | Payout exists: payouts row for job with status = 'paid' | ✅ Optional; or treat job_release as settled. |
